This is a direct logical consequence of the premise.\n\nStep 3: From the premise \"Peter's pets are all either monkeys or birds,\" we know that Rock can either be a monkey or a bird. This premise categorizes Peter's pets into two exclusive groups: monkeys and birds.\n\nStep 4: From the premise \"Peter's birds can fly,\" we know that if Rock is a bird, then Rock can fly. This provides a condition for Rock being a bird.\n\nStep 5: From the premise \"All animals that are Peter's pets can breathe,\" we know that Rock, as one of Peter's pets, can breathe.
